  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_88a12bd9-f0d1-4ebf-9119-d2ce13579afb'

<span id="freeTextContainer9274961200789596108">In the sequel, The Feds' Folly, Who Stole $17 Trillion?, Jones, surviving his jet's bomb related crash, along with his girlfriend Mary, are "on the lam" eluding "hit squads" in the US, Mexico, Costa Rica, and England.   <span id="freeText9274961200789596108" style="display:none">In the sequel, The Feds' Folly, Who Stole $17 Trillion?, Jones, surviving his jet's bomb related crash, along with his girlfriend Mary, are "on the lam" eluding "hit squads" in the US, Mexico, Costa Rica, and England. They leverage damaging inside information provided by a Treasury mole to formulate an elaborate, albeit illegal, plan. If successful, their plan will not only expose the Feds' $17 trillion heist to the world, but it will also bring down the corrupt Swamp Rats in DC, and may even possibly exonerate Jones and his associates.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2508993518" />
    <a title="My World of Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/78838161-my-world-of-reviews"><img alt="My World of Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520362273p2/78838161.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2508993518?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="My World of Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="My World of Reviews" href="/user/show/78838161-my-world-of-reviews">My World of Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2508993518" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3510509763882294501">Mr. Jones and Mary, the two main protagonists of this incredible novel of escape and survival fill the pages from start to finish with their struggle to evade the governmental criminals that are hot on their heels to shut them up permanently for what they know. They take cabs, rent out cottages, put on disguises and use burner phones to survive in what they call the most horrifying crime in the USA that could bring about World War III if what they know hit the worldwide media. The criminals are </span>
  <span id="freeText3510509763882294501" style="display:none">Mr. Jones and Mary, the two main protagonists of this incredible novel of escape and survival fill the pages from start to finish with their struggle to evade the governmental criminals that are hot on their heels to shut them up permanently for what they know. They take cabs, rent out cottages, put on disguises and use burner phones to survive in what they call the most horrifying crime in the USA that could bring about World War III if what they know hit the worldwide media. The criminals are those who have huge positions in financial institutions and federal agencies that have ties to Congress and the President.<br /><br />I found this novel to be so exciting that I finished it in just two days. It kept me up all night just flipping through my kindle eager to find out what the protagonists’ next move will be and if they will be caught by the hit squads that their enemies have hired to hunt them down or what. I recommend this great read to those looking for something concise and eventful to take up their weekend or this last week of summer 2018 coming up. I enjoyed it very much and I am positive that those who will give it a chance will do the same. What a great read! No explicit sexual content, no graphic violence just a bit of blood and injury from a plane crash at the very beginning of this novel. I have to forewarn you that this is the second book in this series and I honestly haven’t read the first part yet. Just a last note: you will not need to read the first part though as this part stands on its own merit. Yes!<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2500612661?book_show_action=true">Aug 20, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Valery" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Valery" href="/user/show/4013735-valery">Valery</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2500612661" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer127936386070628580">The Feds' Folly: Who Stole 17 Trillion? (The Jones Series, Volume 2) by Bill Brown starts off as a follow up to the author's successful novel, Money to Burn. The Feds' Folly however, could easily stand on its own as the author re-introduces us to Jones and his girlfriend Mary. With breathtaking action on the first few pages, with a plane crash and Jones wondering where he is and how he will survive, the story commences with a fast pace. Jones and Mary are not ordinary people however, they are ru</span>
  <span id="freeText127936386070628580" style="display:none">The Feds' Folly: Who Stole 17 Trillion? (The Jones Series, Volume 2) by Bill Brown starts off as a follow up to the author's successful novel, Money to Burn. The Feds' Folly however, could easily stand on its own as the author re-introduces us to Jones and his girlfriend Mary. With breathtaking action on the first few pages, with a plane crash and Jones wondering where he is and how he will survive, the story commences with a fast pace. Jones and Mary are not ordinary people however, they are running for their lives after they uncover a conspiracy of the highest order in the federal government. They must expose the corruption before it is too late and before they lose their lives. Brown writes with a clear voice, setting the scenes well, and giving the characters some depth. You feel the energy and urgency in the story. Overall, a substantial follow up novel in the Jones series, looking forward to more from this author. Highly recommend. </span>
  <a data-text-id="127936386070628580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2543981438" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2543981438" />
    <a title="Lust for Lit" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74624063-lust-for-lit"><img alt="Lust for Lit" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512485063p2/74624063.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2543981438?book_show_action=true">Sep 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lust for Lit" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lust for Lit" href="/user/show/74624063-lust-for-lit">Lust for Lit</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2543981438" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3510359355795029613">Bill Brown amps up the action with his second instalment in 'The Jones' series. 'The Feds Folly' has an adrenaline-fuelled plot that is full of adventure, tension and absolutely thrilling action. We join Mrs. Jones and Mary as they evade shady government agents who aim to silence them for good and frame them for a crime they didn't commit. How can two people (even with their particular set of skills) bring down a corrupt government faction, whilst evading hit men the Feds, and a whole host of ot</span>
  <span id="freeText3510359355795029613" style="display:none">Bill Brown amps up the action with his second instalment in 'The Jones' series. 'The Feds Folly' has an adrenaline-fuelled plot that is full of adventure, tension and absolutely thrilling action. We join Mrs. Jones and Mary as they evade shady government agents who aim to silence them for good and frame them for a crime they didn't commit. How can two people (even with their particular set of skills) bring down a corrupt government faction, whilst evading hit men the Feds, and a whole host of other adversaries? Did I also mention that there is a plane crash? Will they expose the biggest conspiracy America has ever seen or is it all over for Mr. Jones and Mary?<br /><br />I really love the old-school espionage vibes this series has and it is absolutely thrilling from start to finish. I would recommend reading Book 1 'Money to Burn' beforehand if you can, as it is also a cracking novel, but it is not necessary as 'The Feds Folly' stands well on its own.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3510359355795029613" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4Q9a+kEdWeEqOlWrB8E/dh2RQQw0NkZvc8Kcxu4JvKgObB0+4/GtmJEFjnLR/KFpmpNvLPRRPpxbOyH1q9CVlA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ulYnUNLXQiy5NQCPt8bMcOJ/e4HzxznrRmQIH8nNgJxVNWCUcDu2VQIK21Zh+1JvZX1VoTOgQRhunbUsjBSpoA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer6781873945185151554">North Carolina native, Bill Brown, a serial entrepreneur since his UNC '63 days, was always ahead of the curve as the owner and publisher of the Carolina Financial Times, a weekly newspaper, as a co-founder of the Waffle Shoppe restaurant chain, as a principal in a commercial real estate company that developed shopping center sites across the state, and as the major shareholder and president of a </span>
  <span id="freeText6781873945185151554" style="display:none">North Carolina native, Bill Brown, a serial entrepreneur since his UNC '63 days, was always ahead of the curve as the owner and publisher of the Carolina Financial Times, a weekly newspaper, as a co-founder of the Waffle Shoppe restaurant chain, as a principal in a commercial real estate company that developed shopping center sites across the state, and as the major shareholder and president of a company that was the forerunner in the high tech satellite imagery industry. His array of experiences have provided him with some very useful content for all three novels in the Jones Series; Money to Burn, The Feds' Folly, and Delete! </span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_55058686').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_55058686').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_55058686').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
